              <h2 class="block-title">
               <span>

            <div class="spotlight-secondary">
             <a class="comp block no-image" data-doc-id="" href="https://www.thoughtco.com/jesus-before-he-came-to-earth-4157459" id="block_2-0">
              <div class="block-content">
               <p class="block-kicker">

               </p>
               <h2 class="block-title">
                <span>

                </span>
               </h2>
              </div>
             </a>
             <!-- end: comp block no-image -->
             <a class="comp block no-image" data-doc-id="" href="https://www.thoughtco.com/book-of-habakkuk-4155735" id="block_2-0">
              <div class="block-content">
               <p class="block-kicker">
                Article
               </p>
               <h2 class="block-title">
                <span>
                 Introduction to the Book of Habakkuk
                </span>
